msg:We chose to travel on May Day. The size of the parent-child room is 70 square meters, and the configuration is also good. It can be seen that the configuration was quite high when it was renovated before. The hair dryer is very easy to use. The wind is strong but does not hurt the hair. I am very satisfied with this. Maybe because there are so many people, the sanitation is not very satisfactory, especially the side of the bed in the parent-child room, which is not cleaned very cleanly. There is a lot of dust in the places that are basically untouchable. If you don't bring children, it is not recommended to stay in the parent-child room or make a note in advance. Don't use the parent-child bedding. Personally, I think his bedding has faded and looks very dirty, which affects the perception and use. It is better to use pure white. The breakfast is quite good. The overall taste is online. There are multiple breads in the pastry area but no cakes. There is no swimming pool, but the gym is open. The room is close to the main road cross, and there are many large cars passing by at night. The sound insulation effect is not good. It is recommended to wear earplugs. The advantage is that it is very close to Yuantouzhu, Taihu Lake, and you can walk there. The scenery and environment of the riverside trail at the door are very good, which is super suitable for walking. Special thanks to the front desk manager Huang Chunyan for her excellent service. When checking out, she asked if I was satisfied and made corresponding compensation after I reflected the situation. I think this is a very positive attitude and deserves recognition. It can be seen that the hotel is still working hard to adjust after the epidemic. I wish it gets better and better.

Manager Chunyan contacted me as soon as possible and returned the important items I left in time through SF Express. I felt very warm-hearted. Her service was very thoughtful and enthusiastic. Secondly, the location of the hotel is very good. It is right by the Taihu Lake. The scenery is beautiful. It takes only 5 minutes to walk to the Taihu Lake. There are battery cars on the Taihu Lake that can be taken directly to Yuantouzhu. It costs 20 yuan per person, which is very convenient. You can see Yuantouzhu directly from the window of the room. Thirdly, the hotel buffet breakfast is very rich, all the special snacks of Wuxi are available, and the taste is also very good. The hotel service is also very perfect and in place. The guest rooms are cleaned neatly and cleanly, and they are responsive and timely. In addition, the hotel lobby is decorated in the cherry blossom season, which is very suitable for the occasion and can be used for blockbuster photos! The children took a lot of photos in the lobby. This trip was very happy because the thoughtful service of a hotel made me fall in love with the city of Wuxi. Thank you Ruiting Xijiao Hotel and Manager Huang Chunyan. I will choose to stay here next time I come to Wuxi!
